Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

[LGBRC Rides] Sunday Gravel Ride on December 22nd

Dear fellow teammates, Notice that this is a parallel ride to the regular Sunday road ride offered by the club. Plan is to do a long gravel ride along two iconic parks: Calero and QuickSilver. The ride will be a bit demanding, so please do not forget to bring lots of food and water. Also notice that this ride may be cancelled in case of rain or wet terrain. As always we will be regrouping on top of the main climbs and at the bottom of the technical descent. As always, if you are planning on joining it would be great if you could RSVP on the Strava event, so that I can keep you updated on any changes of plan. Also feel free to contact me in private for more info or to coordinate the ride.

Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

Endurance Training Ride

The proposed route is Mt Hamilton all the way out to Patterson and back. Depending on how the group feels and the weather we can assess fatigue at the top of Hamilton, and at The Junction before heading all the way into Patterson. The target pace is to finish in 8-10hrs. This is a strict no-drop ride as the route is very remote and the riders should stick together to support one another in the event of a crash or severe mechanical. With that said, if you struggle to get up Hamilton in 2.5hrs I may ask you to turn back as it will be hard to finish the ride in the time window. Be self-sufficient with navigation, basic repair supplies, food, and water. Thereâ€™s water at the top of Hamilton and at The Junction. The ride will definitely finish after dark so have lights to descend Hamilton. Feel free to DM me on strava or the club WhatsApp for further details. Wheels roll at 8am

Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

78VP6T 7:45 AM Roll out, and a coffee break for 30-40 minutes ğŸŒ¥ 57f âœ ğŸŒ¤ 79f Distance: â­ï¸â­ï¸ Elevation: ğŸ…¿ï¸ Artic 2626 E Katella Ave, Anaheim, CA 92806 â˜•ï¸ Brew Story (22.43M) 16889 Beach Blvd, Huntington Beach, CA 92647 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

LGBRC Sunday Ride

Hello team, There is a good probability that we will have rain this Sunday. If the forecast shows rain for Sunday morning, this ride will be canceled. In the event that we have dry or dry-ish conditions this Sunday, we will meet at MBLG to head south to climb and descend IBM from the same direction. Before climbing IBM, we will stop for bathroom and water at the top of Mockingbird. Wheels roll at 8:35am sharp.

Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

7:30 AM Roll out, and a coffee break for 30-40 minutes ğŸŒ¥ 52f âœ ğŸŒ¤ 76f Distance: â­ï¸â­ï¸ Elevation: â­ï¸â­ï¸ ğŸ…¿ï¸ Cypress Community Park 255 Visions, Irvine, CA 92620 â˜•ï¸ Oslo Coffee Co (21.23M) 25642 Crown Valley Pkwy Suite E1, Ladera Ranch, CA 92694 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. We head out over Shannon to McKean, with a rest stop at Calero park. We then take Bailey up and around to IBM hill (The A group will stay on Bailey to Metcalf). LGBRC Recruitment Ride (A Route)

This Saturday is our annual recruitment ride. Come ride some of our favorite haunts, then join us for gelato on the club at Dolce Spazio. We head out over Shannon to McKean, with a rest stop at Calero park. We then take Bailey up to the feature climb, Metcalf. After regrouping at the top, weâ€™ll descend the backside and loop back around to IBM hill. After that, we wind our way to Kennedy and head back to the shop. There is also alternate route for those would like to skip the Metcalf loop and go directly to IBM hill.

7:30 AM Roll out, and a coffee break for 30-40 minutes â˜ 58f âœ ğŸŒ¤ 75f Distance - â­ï¸â­ï¸ Elevation- â­ï¸ ğŸ…¿ï¸ Columbus Tustin Park 14652 Prospect Ave, Tustin, CA 92780 â˜•ï¸ Mameya Coffee Roasters (18.95M) 27931 La Paz Rd E, Laguna Niguel, CA 92677 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

AV-C Ride Oct 26th, 2024 - Crestview via Palomar and Woodridge Climb

Meet: 9:00 AM, Leave: 9:15 AM We will be going north Saturday, and the weather forecast looks favorable. We will get up to Crestview via Palomar. There are many turns up Palomar, so just follow the signs to keep on Palomar. We have a very short regroup at the gate and a longer regroup at Crestview Park. We will follow Crestview and then Ralston to Crystal Springs with a connection to Woodridge. We will then go up Woodridge climb and connect with Black Mountain Rd. We will then head back on Skyline-Canada and the last main regroup will be at the Water Temple. Planned Regroups: Mountain Home and 84 (Woodside) Crestview Park Skyline and Golf Course Dr. Water Temple Backyard Brew Non-Members: Alto Velo welcomes non-members to join us on our rides. However, non-members must have a Waiver on file with the club. Filling out the waiver is only required one time per year. Ride Etiquette https://www.altovelo.org/ride-rules

[LGBRC Rides] - Saturday Road Ride on October 26th, 2024

Dear fellow Teammates, Let's be back on the road and let's enjoy HW9 that has been recently reopened! The plan for this weekend is to do a classic loop: up HW9, down bear creek and up Big Basin way. As always, we will stop and regroup at the top of each climb and at the bottom of every descent. Weather forecast looks great and while temperatures will be likely on the high 70s we will probably enjoy lower temperatures while climbing: however, please make sure to bring plenty of water (even though we are planning for at least two water stops), and do not forget to eat constantly. As always, if you are planning on joining it would be great if you could RSVP on the strava event, so that I can keep you updated on any changes of plan. Also feel free to contact me in private for more info or to coordinate the ride.

Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

[LGBRC Rides] - Saturday Gravel Ride on October 19th, 2024

Dear fellow Teammates, The plan for this weekend is to do something different and go for a nice gravel ride: climb El Sereno, and JNT before looping around and come back to LG through the LG Creek trail. As always, we will be stop and regroup at the top of each climb and at the bottom of every descent. Please be gentle with me as I am still new on the dirt :-) Weather forecast looks good, but please make sure to bring plenty of water (even though we are planning for at least two water stops). As always, if you are planning on joining it would be great if you could RSVP on the strava event, so that I can keep you updated on any changes of plan. Also feel free to contact me in private for more info or to coordinate the ride.

LGBRC Sunday Ride

Hi team, This Sunday's ride will approach Hicks Rd. from the South. Wheels will roll at 8:35 and take Shannon to Hicks before heading over Camden and taking the maze to New Almaden. We will stop for water and the bathroom at the New Almaden parking lot before climbing Hicks. We will regroup at the top of Hicks where there is also a bathroom at the Hicks and Umunhum intersection. We'll descend Hicks and head back to MBLG via Shannon and Kennedy.

Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

[LGBRC Rides] - Saturday Road Ride on October 12th, 2024

Dear fellow Teammates, The plan for this weekend is to have a long endurance ride and after climbing Hicks, we will head to Uvas before climbing MetCalf. The plan is to keep the peloton together throughout the all ride, but as always we will stop and regroup at the top of each climb and at the bottom of every descent. Notice that the route is designed for "escapes" in case anyone may like to leave early. Weather forecast looks good, but please make sure to bring plenty of water (even though we are planning for at least two water stops). As always, if you are planning on joining it would be great if you could RSVP on the strava event, so that I can keep you updated on any changes of plan. Also feel free to contact me in private for more info or to coordinate the ride.

Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

Group Road Ride - Up 9, down Redwood Gulch

This route is the clockwise version of the regular Redwood Gulch route (2nd Sunday of the month as of this posting). This gives us an opportunity to climb highway 9. One notable change is the out/back after the decent of Redwood Gulch on Stevens Canyon Rd, this adds an additional 4 miles to the total. Before the intersection with Mt. Eden we will stop at Cooley Picnic Area on the left for bathrooms and water. After a quick stop we continue around the reservoir and then follow neighborhood roads back to Mikeâ€™s Bikes.

9BJ8B4 7:15 AM Roll out, and a coffee break for 30-40 minutes â›… 61f âœ â˜€ï¸ 77f Distance - â­ï¸â­ï¸ Elevation- ğŸ…¿ï¸ Artic 2626 E Katella Ave, Anaheim, CA 92806 â˜•ï¸ Succulent Coffee Roasters (17.59M) 17196 Pacific Coast Hwy, Huntington Beach, CA 92649 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

[LGBRC Rides] - Saturday Road Ride on September 21st, 2024

Dear fellow teammates, As the weekend is approaching, it is time to plan another epic adventure. The plan for Saturday is to climb Mt. Umunhum not once but twice :-) The route is designed for easy escapes in case you may not want to complete the whole quest or simply decide that climbing Mt. Umunhum once would be enough. The forecast is for a warm day, so please do not forget to bring plenty of water and to hydrate yourself during the ride. Also bring lots of food, and do not forget to fuel yourself constantly. Note that this ride will not be about speed, but it is meant to help build endurance and strength. If you have any questions, please do not hesitate to reach out! See you on Saturday!
